    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_85b58c29-0a78-43de-9ade-82744bdadcde'

  <span id="freeText14463047771153768835" style="display:none"><b>Dating the Prince of Darkness has its challenges...</b><br /><br />Leila's psychic abilities have been failing her, and now she isn't sure what the future holds. If that weren't enough, her lover, Vlad, has been acting distant. Though Leila is a mere mortal, she's also a modern woman who refuses to accept the cold shoulder treatment forever–especially from the darkly handsome vampire who still won't admit that he loves her.<br /><br /><b>Like choosing between eternal love and a loveless eternity...</b><br /><br />Soon circumstances send Leila back to the carnival circuit, where tragedy strikes. And when she finds herself in the crosshairs of a killer who may be closer than she realizes, Leila must decide who to trust– the fiery vampire who arouses her passions like no other or the tortured knight who longs to be more than a friend? With danger stalking her every step of the way, all it takes is one wrong move to damn her for eternity.</span>

This question contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a href="/questions/1733342-vlad-leila-are-my-all-time-favorite"><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Vlad&amp;Leila are my all time favorite couple!! (even though book 3 is meh and book 4 is even worse). <br />Why Leila was never angry at Vlad for her kidnapping in book 2? Vlad was very protective of her in book 1. In book 2 he even said that it's dangerous for her to leave. But she was snatched up within a week of returning from Vlad's. He didn't even put guards on her. Doesn't seem like Vlad to just leave her unprotected. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></a>
</span>

<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/50938238-shannon-fay"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1451740716i/50938238._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/50938238-shannon-fay">Shannon Fay</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    Because if you remember, after that huge explosion in the tunnel, they though Szilagyi was dead (since he isn't fireproof), and that he wasn't going t<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    Because if you remember, after that huge explosion in the tunnel, they though Szilagyi was dead (since he isn't fireproof), and that he wasn't going to come after her anymore. And technically he didn't do that himself, it was someone else that blew her up. So he thought that since Szilagyi was dead, Leila wasn't under threat anymore, so there wasn't anything for her to be afraid of, which is why he just let her go. Plus, I think he was very hurt that she did actually leave and wasn't thinking 100% clearly. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2259618858847927565"><b>5 Mrs. Dracula Stars</b><br/><br/>First read 3/4/2014 Reread 12/5/2015 Re reread 11/30/2019<br/><br/><b>*Spoilers*</b><br/><br/><b>"The dress, the fancy dinner, all your flattering words, then the jewelry box." I ticked the items off on my fingers. "Really, what was I supposed to think?" His snort cut me to the bone. "Anything but that. You and I have been together mere months. Do you know how insignificant that is to someone my age?" A fresh wave of hurt made my tone scalding. "Yes, you're almost six hundred years old, but in today's wor</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2259618858847927565" style="display:none"><b>5 Mrs. Dracula Stars</b><br><br>First read 3/4/2014 Reread 12/5/2015 Re reread 11/30/2019<br><br><b>*Spoilers*</b><br><br><b>"The dress, the fancy dinner, all your flattering words, then the jewelry box." I ticked the items off on my fingers. "Really, what was I supposed to think?" His snort cut me to the bone. "Anything but that. You and I have been together mere months. Do you know how insignificant that is to someone my age?" A fresh wave of hurt made my tone scalding. "Yes, you're almost six hundred years old, but in today's world, when you say things like 'eternal bond' before giving your girlfriend a ring-sized box, there's usually only one kind of ring in it!"-Leila and Vlad</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9260148_zpsoem8wui9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449365185ra/17276079.gif" alt=" photo 9260148_zpsoem8wui9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> "It hurts too much to be close to you, but continually pushed away." His expression changed to disbelief. "You're leaving me?"-Leila and Vlad</b> <br><br>Twice Tempted , the 2nd book in the Night Prince Series, was better then the first. And that is saying a lot because the first one was awesome! So much happens in this book. Wow lets just see if I can remember to name it all. Okay so the book picks up right where the last one left off. Leila and Vlad are having problems because Leila is worried that Vlad don't want her anymore because she lost her power( they don't know if it's temporary or not) Vlad tries to show Leila that he still wants her by giving her his sire line ring (meaning he wants to turn her into a vampire) at a fancy dinner in front of a lot of people which lead to Leila and Vlad having a huge embarrassing misunderstanding that leads to them breaking up. <br><br><b> Tell me you love me and I'll stay. Hell, tell me you'll be open to the IDEA of loving me and I'll stay. Tell me anything except to resign myself to always ranking a distant second to the coldness you keep wrapping around your heart.-Leila</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/klhgi_zpsbdxffkvr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449365185i/17276080.jpg" alt=" photo klhgi_zpsbdxffkvr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"In the past month, I've been rejected, blown up, shot at, drugged, and kidnapped, but I'd rather go through all of that again than hold your hand while acting like . . . like everything that happened between us doesn't matter." My voice cracked. "Maybe it doesn't to you, but even being around you hurts and I can't pretend that touching you won't be a thousand times worse."-Leila</b><br><br><br>Leila leaves Vlad and goes back to stay with Marty. Then someone tries to kill Leila, Maximus saves Leila then they try to find who tried to kill her. Then she and Maximus get kidnapped. Then she kicks some major ass and gets ahold of Vlad to help. Then her and Vlad get back together. Then they get married! Then someone tries to kill her a few more times. Then she dies and becomes a vampire. Then there is some awesomely dirty blood sex........(they are so naughty) Then they hunt down the people that tried to kill Leila. I think I got it all! Pfff See a lot happened!<br><br><br><b>"I'd want our wedding to be special. I don't have a dress, you don't have a best man, and instead of flowers, we have corpses on poles decorating the front of the house." "Flowers are on the way, as is my best man, three seamstresses are ready to make any dress you desire, and I'll have the corpses taken down," he replied without missing a beat.-Leila and Vlad<br><br><br>My father cast a calculated look at the items on the silver serving tray in front of him. Vlad flashed him a charming smile. "You'd never succeed." For a second, I didn't understand. Then my mouth fell open. "Dad! You were not thinking of stabbing my fiance with a silver knife!"-Vlad and Leila<br><br><br>"You think I object because he's a vampire?" my father snapped. "If you were marrying Marty, I'd give my blessing because he's a good man. He" - a finger stabbed in Vlad's direction - "is not." I sighed. "You saw the corpses on the lawn, didn't you?" My father let out a scoff. "As if I couldn't tell before that. I told you, Leila, I can read people, and without a doubt, Vlad is the most violent person I've ever met."-Leila's dad and Leila</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/TwiceTempted-Sb-for-blog1_zpst2lbbn0h.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449365185i/17276081._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo TwiceTempted-Sb-for-blog1_zpst2lbbn0h.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Yesterday, I woke up in the infirmary still nursing a broken heart. Today, I woke up in Vlad's bed as Mrs. Dracula. What a difference a day made. "If you introduce yourself to anyone as Mrs. Dracula, I'll bite you in a manner you won't enjoy." I smiled without opening my eyes. Some things didn't change, like Vlad being grumpy when he first woke up. "I'm quaking with fear." -Leila and Vlad</b><br><br>At the start of the book I have to say I was so embarrassed for Leila. I actually felt it. I think I blushed and everything. And Vlad I wanted to kick his ass. He was so stupid not to see how that ring party would look. But when they got back together Vlad melted my heart and made me fall in love with his complex, dark self all over again. The thing I love about Vlad is that even though he falls in love it doesn't change who he is. He is still Vlad to his core. I love him and Leila together. I love that Leila doesn't back down to Vlad either. Vlad is a strong person he could never love a weak person. Poor Vlad I feel bad for him when he was betrayed by a friend. Cat makes a cameo appearance after the wedding which made me miss Bones and Cat. Good thing their book is up next. The story was a great addition to The Night Huntress Universe. If you love PNR or Urban fantasy you should check this whole series out starting with Bones and Cat! <br><br><b>"Love is a terrible weakness. It gives your enemies a perfect target, clouds your judgment, makes you reckless . . . and that's on a good day." His hands continued their caressing path to my waist, their heat barely diminished by the thin material of my robe. "On a bad day," he went on, his voice turning harsh, "it can destroy you. I never wanted to subject myself to that again, so yes, I kept you at arm's length. I even let you leave to prove to myself that you meant no more to me than my previous lovers. And then Martin called, telling me you'd been killed." His grip tightened painfully before he released me, his hands clenching into fists at his sides. "I didn't care about anything then. Not crushing my enemies, protecting my people, or how maddening you were by expecting me to behave like a modern man, as if I could shrug off half a millennium of living, based on your whim."-Vlad<br><br><br><br>"This place stinks." "Did the guards forget to spray Febreze?" Vlad asked in mock indignation. Then he gave me a jaded look. "It's a dungeon, Leila. They're supposed to smell." Mission accomplished. The stench might have actually killed my new appetite. If Hell could fart, it would smell like this.-Leila and Vlad</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3580725490799433380">Jerk<br/>Ruthless<br/>Sardonic <br/>Heartless<br/>Cold<br/>Distant<br/>Manipulative<br/>Cruel<br/><br/>In short Vlad was pretty much an ass in this book. To those who only read Night Prince they would see him that way but I've read the entire Night Huntress Series and Night Huntress World so I kind of know where he was coming from. Quite frankly I'm a little disappointed because I felt he lost some of his edge. I thought he became soft. Hehe Leila got to him.<br/><br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ <br/>The marriage thing was a little too soon for me but who am I? Vlad</span></span>
  <span id="freeText3580725490799433380" style="display:none">Jerk<br />Ruthless<br />Sardonic <br />Heartless<br />Cold<br />Distant<br />Manipulative<br />Cruel<br /><br />In short Vlad was pretty much an ass in this book. To those who only read Night Prince they would see him that way but I've read the entire Night Huntress Series and Night Huntress World so I kind of know where he was coming from. Quite frankly I'm a little disappointed because I felt he lost some of his edge. I thought he became soft. Hehe Leila got to him.<br /><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br />The marriage thing was a little too soon for me but who am I? Vlad did it to please Leila, some kind of human formality thing.<br /><br />I also felt bad for Vlad because he lost two of his closest friends. I was getting the traitor vibe from Maximus but Shrapnel? I didn't see that one coming. Too bad, I really liked him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Leila was even more stubborn in this book. My goodness, sometimes it was a little too much. How many times did she almost die in this book? She also became clingy which kind of irked my irritation, however, she still kicks major butt. Go girl.<br /><br />The whole story pretty much revolved around Leila trying to stay "alive", Vlad trying to save her, accept as well as admit his feelings and the blossoming of their relationship (blossoming? wtf?). <br /><br />Lastly, Yay for book 3! I think this was supposed to be a 2-book thing but hah! This book didn't even show the main baddie so I'm hoping that the 3rd book would have action packed butt kicking.<br /><br />------------------------------------------------------------<br />On a completely unrelated note, Up From the Grave is next. <b> Hoorah! </b> I miss Cat and Bones, they'll always be number one. :) I couldn't even read the excerpt, don't wanna torture myself with it. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11694991566439333615">You know, Vlad was just so awesome in this one. However, I can already see him slipping into Frost's default "whatever you wish, darling" male characters. I would really like if the character remained mostly the same as they were before meeting their love. But I wish the ending wasn't so fast. It ended when it was finally interesting;). <br/>Wonder when we will see Maximus again.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16421192531554250660"><b>Once burned....twice tempted</b><br/><br/>So good!<br/><br/>Leila is furious!<br/>Maybe it is because Leila has lost her “gift” and she feels helpless....<br/>Maybe it is because Vlad does not seem to care for her needs (There is no bathroom in his room!)... <br/>Maybe it is because Vlad wants to make her a vampire (Doesn't he like the fact that she is a puny human?)...<br/>Maybe it is because this wedding proposal is not offered...<br/>...So...Leila leaves Vlad and surprisingly Vlad lets her abandoning him.<br/><br/>Leila goes back at US, but Martin ha</span>
  <span id="freeText16421192531554250660" style="display:none"><b>Once burned....twice tempted</b><br /><br />So good!<br /><br />Leila is furious!<br />Maybe it is because Leila has lost her “gift” and she feels helpless....<br />Maybe it is because Vlad does not seem to care for her needs (There is no bathroom in his room!)... <br />Maybe it is because Vlad wants to make her a vampire (Doesn't he like the fact that she is a puny human?)...<br />Maybe it is because this wedding proposal is not offered...<br />...So...Leila leaves Vlad and surprisingly Vlad lets her abandoning him.<br /><br />Leila goes back at US, but Martin has already found a replacement, new enemies appear and some old friends -although they seem like they want to help- cannot be trusted (Maximus, what are you trying to do?). Leila is penniless and desperate.<br /><br />Has Vlad really let her leave him?<br /><br /><i>“You should be afraid. Very afraid. Before, I told you if you wanted to end things between us, I would let you go, but, Leila"--his voice deepened--"I lied.” </i><br /><br />This is another incredible book! It has everything: angst, mystery, desperation, bad and not so bad vampires, unconditional love and finally a first-class, amazing wedding with many friends.<br /><br />Vlad and Leila, congratulations!<br /><br /><i>“As if I'd settle for anything less than making you completely mine, as soon as possible.”<br />He was so close his features were a blur, yet his eyes had never gleamed brighter. I closed mine and it made no difference. I could still see his through the shield of my lids.<br />"I am yours," I whispered, and it wasn't only a statement. It was a promise.</i></span>

<div id="review_521928641" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/521928641" />
    <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth"><img alt="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487525094p2/13870608.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/521928641?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo ★The Book Sloth★" href="/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth">Jo ★The Book Sloth★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer521928641" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5770666271349396686">I really, really don't know what to do with this book... I can't even decide how to rate it (I change my mind every ten minutes). It had moments where I wanted to clap my hands and have a little happy dance and then I'd read something and want to close the book and save myself the disappointment. I wanted to cry at some points because all my expectations turned to dust!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/522333.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>*****SPOILERS*****</u>
</b><br/><br/>I'd decided I wouldn't use spoilers for this one but I don't know how to do it and explain at the same tim</span>
  <span id="freeText5770666271349396686" style="display:none">I really, really don't know what to do with this book... I can't even decide how to rate it (I change my mind every ten minutes). It had moments where I wanted to clap my hands and have a little happy dance and then I'd read something and want to close the book and save myself the disappointment. I wanted to cry at some points because all my expectations turned to dust!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/522333.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>*****SPOILERS*****</u>
</b><br><br>I'd decided I wouldn't use spoilers for this one but I don't know how to do it and explain at the same time why I was disappointed, so spoilers it is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407477ra/795873.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will begin by saying that this Vlad has nothing to do with the Vlad from Night Huntress, he doesn't even resemble the more mundane edition of him from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7039218.Once_Burned__Night_Prince___1_" title="Once Burned (Night Prince, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Once Burned</a>. I want the unyielding, arrogant, heartless, full of dark humor SOB he once was back.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This Vlad was wrapped around Leila's finger for the better part of the book like a schoolboy with his first crush. He kept threatening her with ramifications to her decisions, and then he forgave her every time. As if that wasn't enough, he had to go out of his way to give her everything she wanted in the end. And I do mean every single thing, even the ones that he'd promised never to give.<br><br>I can't believe I'm saying it but my favorite moment in the book with him was when he broke Leila's heart. At least at that point he was the Vlad I knew and loved (you know...Cold, cruel, cynical). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I just kept reading and trying to understand who this new hero was and where my Vlad was. The worst drawback in this was that you couldn't see the changes happening. There wasn't a developement period. One day he was cold and heartless and the next he was a mat for Leila to walk all over. I just can't see this happening. Maybe if the changes happened one at a time I could suck it up and say "well, the man fell in love, of course he would change" but it was like he slept one night and woke up another person. I knew that at some point he'd relent, I just wanted to be able to see what led to it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407477ra/795874.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then of course we have Leila. Leila the strong, brave, gutsy heroine of the first book, has become Leila the whiny, naive, needy little girl in the second. What happened to her? So Vlad can't love her, so what?<br><br><b>***NEWS FLASH Girl, you knew that going in. He said he can't love you first thing in the relationship. He never promised you anything. If you want more than he can give you, you man up and leave him.***</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[But nope, not her. She had to become clingy and humiliate both of them before she finally got that he couldn't give her what she wanted. And of course after that she had to believe the worst of him(believe he was capable of some pretty awful things-and willing to do them-) because... well, the only reason I can think of was that did what he had promised from the beginning, protected and sexed her up without promising his undying love. Yeap, I can deffinitely see why she would believe that after he gave her exactly what he promised her, he could do the things she suspects him for. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So what I have to say to Leila is... <br><br><b>Grow up and stop acting like a bratty 15 year old who thinks the world goes in circles around her.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407477ra/795875.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Concerning the book in general, mostly my bigest disappoinment in the book were the characters. That isn't to say that it didn't have it's good moments. Moments when the good, old Vlad we know and love, came out to play. Moments when Leila thought of someone besides herself. But they just couldn't tip the balance with the rest in my opinion. There were also exchanges where the old Vlad (the ruthless, dark one) showed his beautiful self and then, just when you thought the guy still had "it", Leila caught his balls again.<br><br>I don't know if it was the high expectations I had for this one or the anticipation for something good but I was brought down to Earth none too gently.<br><br>The last 1/4 of the book was somewhat better, or at least the action helped to get over the disasters of the first half of the book. I read through the book, praying that my beloved Vlad would come back, but in the end I ended up with "Leila's Man". That's exactly what happened to him, he wasn't Vlad anymore, he was "Leila's man".<br><br>I know the book had good moments. I actually quite enjoyed it at some points but I just can't even remember them right now. My mind has stopped at the bad things and can't get over them.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407477ra/795876.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>PS. Please Frost, give us Vlad back in the next book. PLEASE!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5770666271349396686" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245661990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2233942611271110798"><br/><b>5 Searing Stars!! That's what I’m talking about! BURN BABY BURN…Vlad set me on Fire!! </b><br/><br/><b>FINALLY</b> we get the sexy, snarky Vlad we have come to love from <i>The Night Huntress</i> series! This book was so much better than the first one. Leila grew into her character and Vlad has come back to us!! They will never be Cat and Bones, and I wouldn’t want them to be, but they are a unique fun couple in their own right. The steam factor was off the charts, they don't call him 'The Impaler' for nothing. Actually it</span>
  <span id="freeText2233942611271110798" style="display:none"><br><b>5 Searing Stars!! That's what I’m talking about! BURN BABY BURN…Vlad set me on Fire!! </b><br><br><b>FINALLY</b> we get the sexy, snarky Vlad we have come to love from <i>The Night Huntress</i> series! This book was so much better than the first one. Leila grew into her character and Vlad has come back to us!! They will never be Cat and Bones, and I wouldn’t want them to be, but they are a unique fun couple in their own right. The steam factor was off the charts, they don't call him 'The Impaler' for nothing. Actually it's for other reasons, but in my mind...well you get the picture. I loved the witty banter between Vlad and Leila, which usually led to more impaling! *snicker*<br><br><i>When we entered the first chamber of the dungeon, the stench made me recoil. It smelled like someone had mixed together kerosene, rotten fruit, stale blood, urine, and dog shit, then blown it up. How had I not noticed this before? I wasn’t even breathing, but the rancid odor found its way into my nose anyway. “This place stinks.”<br><br>“Did the guards forget to spray Febreze?” Vlad asked in mock indignation. Then he gave me a jaded look. “It’s a dungeon, Leila. They’re supposed to smell.”</i><br><br>Vlad, he’s so old school and barbaric, yet such a modern man!<br><br>I listened to this book on audio and then went back and read my favorite parts. I love the audio version and Tavia Gilbert does an amazing Vlad, Romanian accent and all! When he says Leila…long and drawn out…Leeiiiiiilaaaa…it just made me melt! <br><br>This book gave me that feeling I had when I first read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1421990.Halfway_to_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___1_" title="Halfway to the Grave (Night Huntress, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Halfway to the Grave</a>. Plenty of action, world-building, fantastic secondary characters, a real page turner! I’m excited to see where this series is going, and I can’t wait to spend more time with Vlad and Leila! Jeaniene Frost, you did good! <br><br>I had a pic I was going to post of Vlad, but when I saw <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/357650859" rel="nofollow noopener">Dorsey’s</a>, I put mine aside because <b>she nailed it </b>!!! This is the picture I will have in my head as I continue to read this series. She also posted some of my favorite quotes and wrote a great review! Our love for Vlad shows no bounds, does it my friend?! We are Vlad groupies! <br><br><b>Dorsey gifted me my own Vlad pic to post on my review!! He's so perfect, thank you my dear sweet friend!! MUAH!!! <br><br>The Impaler ~ Vlad!!! </b><br><a href="http://s1130.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/media/Vlad_zps90805dba.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364722i/716521.jpg" alt=" photo Vlad_zps90805dba.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer11824249912736444390"><i> reread 9/2020 </i><br/><br/>-----------------------------------<br/><br/><b> 4.5 fiery Dracula stars! </b><br/><br/>Loved this Vlad follow up!! Leila and Vlad are my 2nd favorite couple in the Night Huntress World (second only to Cat and Bones of course). Leila is by far the best heroine of the spin-offs. She's a strong, admirable lady and I love that she refuses to be second best in life and stands by her choices.<br/><br/>Great plot, great angst, and a great romance. I highly recommend the Night Prince series and it can be easily read without</span>
  <span id="freeText11824249912736444390" style="display:none"><i> reread 9/2020 </i><br><br>-----------------------------------<br><br><b> 4.5 fiery Dracula stars! </b><br><br>Loved this Vlad follow up!! Leila and Vlad are my 2nd favorite couple in the Night Huntress World (second only to Cat and Bones of course). Leila is by far the best heroine of the spin-offs. She's a strong, admirable lady and I love that she refuses to be second best in life and stands by her choices.<br><br>Great plot, great angst, and a great romance. I highly recommend the Night Prince series and it can be easily read without reading any other connected books (but I still urge you to read Halfway to the Grave first).<br><br>One note, others have said that this Vlad is not the same as the one we met in Cat's books, but I choose to think of him as a different character in this book, so it doesn't bother me as much.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>

  <span id="freeText7678486756742656293" style="display:none">Twice Tempted by Jeaniene Frost<br /><br />Night Prince series, book 2. You should read the prior book for the best context. <br />This book travels far in terms of changes for Leila. At first Leila thinks Vlad is going to propose but when that doesn’t happen, she walks away from him. An attempt is made on her life and then events are happening fast and spinning out of control. <br />Often bloody and violent, the story is full of vampires making their own lives important, even if at the cost of others. But like life, there is good with the bad.<br /><br />I look forward to reading more of this series because: CLIFFHANGER!<br /><br />I alternated between a paperback and audio version narrated by Tavia Gilbert. Tavia does a fantastic job alternating between voices and empathizing passion and anxiety. </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576581389" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576581389?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576581389" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13426504870691972754"><b>Spoilers… A Very Long, Ranty and Disorganised Review</b><br/><br/>What the hell was this? I thought <i>Once Burned</i> was an okay read - it was cliched and predictable but it had its entertaining moments. I obviously didn't expect much from <i>Twice Tempted</i> but I didn't think it'd be this fucking awful. It was positively horrible. <br/><br/>I'm even more pissed because I loved Cat and Bones's books (even though the last few have been boring) and I quite liked Spade and Mencheres's books too. Sadly, Vlad's books make me want to </span>
  <span id="freeText13426504870691972754" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers… A Very Long, Ranty and Disorganised Review</b><br /><br />What the hell was this? I thought <i>Once Burned</i> was an okay read - it was cliched and predictable but it had its entertaining moments. I obviously didn't expect much from <i>Twice Tempted</i> but I didn't think it'd be this fucking awful. It was positively horrible. <br /><br />I'm even more pissed because I loved Cat and Bones's books (even though the last few have been boring) and I quite liked Spade and Mencheres's books too. Sadly, Vlad's books make me want to throw up. It was like no effort or thought or imagination were put into his books. They're bloody awful.<br /><br />I loved Vlad in the <i>Night Huntress</i> series, he was mysterious, attractive, funny and caring. I couldn't wait to read his spin-off. Unfortunately, he turned into a dull, cliched loser. I could have coped with that if not for the fact that he was paired with a boring clingy doormat who had no self respect. Ugh. <br /><br />Leila was kind of blah in the first book but in this one she was down right annoying. I was hoping she would drop dead and Vlad's vampires would just dump her in a dustbin… And then maybe Vlad could disappear for a century or two to cleanse himself of all that Leila awfulness so he could return with an actual personality. No such luck though.<br /><br />The worst thing about <i>Twice Tempted</i> was Vlad and Leila. They were boring, insufferable, cliched, pathetic, lame, rubbish and cringey.<br /><br />If I was Leila I would have stopped whining and told Vlad to fuck off, then had sex with that other vampire bloke and kept him on the side for his super healing blood, and then joined the carnival again and become a free loving hippie. Did Leila do that? No, she just whined and moaned like a cow.<br /><br />If I was Vlad, I would have impaled Leila and not in a sexy way. I would have used dozens of metal pikes to slowly kill her. <br />What did Vlad see in Leila? She was the worst. <br /><br />I think that Leila just wore Vlad down and forced him into having feelings for her. I don't think Vlad truly loved Leila, she was unloveable and he treated her like shit for too long to make me believe he loved her.<br /><br /><u>A breakdown of Vlad and Leila's relationship</u>:<br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> I love you so so so so so so so much. Do you be also loving me?<br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> No.<br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> Please please pwease be wuving me. Me no like how you torture people. It no nice. I loving you lots yea? You please loving me? Thank you, please.<br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> No. Fuck off.<br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> I go now. Remember I be always loving you. I no be loving you being the cold torturer bastard but I still loving you.<br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> That makes no sense. <br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> Vlad being so evul and mean. I love him so so much. What do now?<br /><br /><b>Other Vampire Dude:</b> Vlad is despicable. Why on earth do you love him?<br /><br /><b>Leila</b>: You no understand. I hate him because he evul but I love him, all of him. Why no-one understand that? It being so simple. I love the Vlad but I hate the Vlad personality. You see why I loving him?!<br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> I built you a toilet. Let's get married.<br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> A toilet and a marriage? A toilet must be meaning you loving me. All I ever being wanted is the toilet. <br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> I bought you toilet paper too.<br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> I being the luckiest girl in the whole widest world!! I be getting a toilet and a toilet paper that be meaning I being the loved like no other. All other girl being jealous of my toilet. <br /><br /><b>Leila:</b> Vlad, come! Come watching me on the toilet machine! Look what I do!<br /><br /><b>Vlad:</b> Ugh.<br /><br />Fin.<br /><br /><b>Other Random Thoughts:</b><br /><br />-Leila leaves Vlad because she's a loser and he's a douche. She goes back to her carnie life and mates and then someone blows up her trailer. Naturally, Leila puts on her Mary Sue knickers and investigates. Yes, it was as boring as it sounds.<br /><br />-Leila's voice and attitude was beyond irritating. She sounded like a tween girl instead of a grown woman. She said things like: <br />Yuck, this days sucks, Eat me! TMI, If Hell could fart, it would smell like this, I was chillaxin’. <br />And she also burped in a vampire's face… She was so immature and childish. <br />And the way Leila kept monologuing about how slutty she was really pissed me off. The silly cow has only had one sexual partner yet she calls herself slutty! <br /><br />-I was sick of Leila's inner fucking voice. I felt like I was reading 50 Shades of Grey. Oooh my inner voice said this and oooh my inner voice is saying that now. It wasn't cute or endearing, it was just annoying.<br /><br />-How dumb was Vlad when he made a big song and dance about Leila and then presented her with something that looked like an engagement ring box? Of course, she would have thought he was proposing! He was so thick. And why would he even offer to make her a vampire without discussing it with her first? It was dumb.<br />And Leila was just as stupid. Why would she get happy that he was 'proposing' when they'd only been dating for a few months and when Vlad hadn't even told her he loved her? What a silly cow.<br /><br />-I thought it was dumb that Leila didn't clock on to the fact that her 'dreams' of Vlad were actually real. It was so fucking obvious.<br /><br />-I think Leila only loved Vlad because he was powerful, attractive and immune to her powers. It was a shallow and superficial love.<br /><br />-Why the fuck was there a description of a love triangle in the synopsis? It was the lamest love triangle ever. It wasn't even a love triangle.<br />Maximus never stood a chance. Leila was obsessed with Vlad, she wasn't torn about who she wanted. Maximus wasn't even competition for Vlad. Lame. The synopsis is misleading, I was expecting a love triangle but got nothing.<br /><br />-Leila's thoughts were similar to a tween girl with a crush. It was all so cringey, pathetic, cheesy, cliched and desperate. Leila was boring as fuck. What does Vlad see in her?<br />I lost all respect for Leila when she was begging Vlad to love her, and I hated her when she said she'd stay with him if he could one day possibly love her. WTF?! Basically she would have stayed with him for years loving him and not being loved back because there was a small chance he might one day love her. Ugh. Have some self respect girl!<br /><br />-It was obvious that Vlad never loved Leila. He was always cold to her, plus it took him ages to build her that fucking toilet she wanted!<br /><br />-I can't buy the love between a hero and heroine when the hero watches the heroine suffering because he refuses to say he loves her.<br />If he had loved her he wouldn't have hurt her or watched her be in pain, all because he couldn't say three fucking words.<br />Vlad being occasionally growly and possessive doesn't translate into love.<br /><br />-If Leila's life hadn't been threatened would Vlad have even bothered with her again? No. She would have grown old, bitter and alone dreaming about Vlad and Vlad would have just replaced her with another lover<br /><br />-Vlad pushed Leila so far that she had to use her powers to prove that she loved him… which led to her dying. Bones/Mencheres/Spade would never make Cat/Kira/Denise feel so shit that they felt like they had to kill themselves to show that they were worthy of Bones and co's love. Vlad only gave Leila the time of day because she killed herself for him.<br />Bones and co can show affection and softness when they're around Cat and co but does Vlad show any affection towards Leila? No, he treats her like he treats everyone else, like shit. When he's with Leila he just acts a little more hornier… Yet I'm meant to believe Vlad's deeply in love with Leila?! How is being horny and kind of possessive love?!<br /><br />-I think Leila and Vlad have some feelings for each other but I don't believe that they're each others one true love or whatever. I think that Leila loves him in a way a tween girl loves their favourite pop star… And I think Vlad has some feelings for her because 1. She was a virgin when he fucked her and 2. He's intrigued by her unique powers.<br /> <br />-Vlad's true love was his first wife — he was mourning her for centuries and he's never gotten over her, and her death changed him completely… Leila has never and will never elicit those sort of feelings and change in Vlad. <br />I actually wish Vlad's HEA could have been with his reincarnated first wife or something — maybe then he'd be a more three dimensional character instead of the caricature that he is.<br /><br />-I don't find Vlad's flat, dark, cliched, cold, broody personality attractive AT ALL - maybe with his first wife he could have shown a different side and shown some depth to his character. Instead he's with boring pathetic desperate Leila who he either ignores, belittles or acts possessive or lusty towards. And that's not enough for me to believe that he 1. Loves her and 2. Has a layered and complex personality.<br /><br />-I found Vlad's sudden commitment to Leila bizarre. One minute he was cold and uninterested and the next he wanted marriage and couldn't stop saying I love you to Leila. It was dumb and I didn't buy what Vlad was saying because there was very little evidence to support his I love you's.<br /><br />-The wedding was rubbish — there was nothing romantic about it, probably because it was rushed and because Vlad and Leila's love was shallow at best.<br /> <br />-It was grating how Leila described Vlad every time she saw him. I already know he's fit and wears sexy clothes. I don't need to be told a thousand bloody times. <br /><br />-I was pissed that Leila was treated like shit by all of Vlad's vampires as soon as she broke up with him. She thought they were her friends but they turned their backs on her as soon as she wasn't fucking Vlad… Basically all her friendships with Vlad's vampires were false and reliant on Leila being Vlad's girlfriend… Nice. <br />The only reason the other vampires are friendly to her at the end was because she was with Vlad again. So Leila has to live centuries with a bunch of vampires who only pretend to like her because she's dating Vlad. What a bunch of fuckers.<br /><br />-Leila treated Maximus like shit. Marty and Maximus were the only decent characters.<br /><br />-I got sick of Leila talking about her twagic scar. Get over it! She acted like she was disfigured and ugly... She obviously wasn't. Loads of fit guys fancied her and it couldn't have been for her rubbish personality so it must have been because she was gorgeous. Oh boo hoo, poor Leila has a little scar on her beautiful face. Ugh.<br /><br />-Leila's sister and dad treated her like shit. They've not been a part of her life for years and they've shown no interest in her but as soon as she becomes a part of the vampire world, they're all up in her arse.<br />I liked that Leila's sister slapped her though, I would have liked it more if her sister wasn't such an awful character.<br /><br />-Ugh. Really? The cliched jealous ex-girlfriend that can't get over the hero because he's just that desirable. Give me a break.<br /><br />-The characters were cliched, the writing was flat and the story was predictable and dull.<br /><br />Skip Vlad's books because they're utter rubbish. It's filled with one dimensional characters, a loveless and passionless romance and an unimaginative story. <br />If you want to read a half decent vampire romance then read Cat/Bones's, Spade/Denise's and Kira/Mencheres's books… They're not perfect but unlike <i>Twice Tempted</i>, they are romantic and fun.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13426504870691972754" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_478405385" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478405385" />
    <a title="La-Lionne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne"><img alt="La-Lionne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458815714p2/11644154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478405385?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="La-Lionne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="La-Lionne" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne">La-Lionne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=dumb-heroine">dumb-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=just-blah">just-blah</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=skipped-a-lot">skipped-a-lot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=could-not-finish">could-not-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=disappointing-sequel">disappointing-sequel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478405385" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13095398133571948733">I still don't understand what happened to the characters I met in the first book.<br/>I really enjoyed the first book. I liked both Vlad and Leila. I loved the whole mystery surrounding his character, his darkness, his arrogance and his possessive unapologetic behavior. I loved Leila's innocence, her bravery and her struggle to understand and control her powers. I also like that she feared him, but at the same time felt this uncontrollable pull towards him. <br/><br/>But in this book I almost didn't recognized</span>
  <span id="freeText13095398133571948733" style="display:none">I still don't understand what happened to the characters I met in the first book.<br />I really enjoyed the first book. I liked both Vlad and Leila. I loved the whole mystery surrounding his character, his darkness, his arrogance and his possessive unapologetic behavior. I loved Leila's innocence, her bravery and her struggle to understand and control her powers. I also like that she feared him, but at the same time felt this uncontrollable pull towards him. <br /><br />But in this book I almost didn't recognized her. She was whiny, demanding, constantly nagging him. What I dislike the most about this book was the fact that she made her decisions based on assumptions instead of actual facts. <br /><br />For me, the story started to go south pretty early in the book.<br /><br />- WARNING SPOILERS -<br /><br />The whole scene with the ring was ridiculous. I understand why she would assume that, but her reaction to it was very childish. First of all, if there was anything to be pissy about it was the fact that he wanted to turn her into a vampire. But she didn't dwell on it for very long. She started to nag him why he haven't said I love you to her. Let's back up a little. When she first saw the jewelry box she started to squirm in her seat and couldn't wait to say "yes" even without his I love you, so why complain about it afterwards?<br />Vlad have lived, loved, hated, suffered and killed for hundreds of years. He's a vampire who doesn't live by our mortal rules. I would say she had a thing or two to learn from him. I was on his side when it came to the whole I love you thing. <br /><br />"Words." His tone sharpened. "I shared my house, my bed, and my blood with you, as well as offered you a place in my life forever. What are words compared to that?"<br /><br />He was trying to tell her that actions speak louder than words, which is true, but she was still stomping her foot and pushing him to tell her that he loved her. And when he didn't she told him it was over. It was so annoying. <br /><br />Another thing that I didn't like was cartoon-like descriptions. Which made it hard for me to get into the story and take it seriously. Leila comparing the remains on a deck to a lasagna and the crime scene at the hotel she compared to a Swiss cheese. You've got to be kidding me? I expected to be scared, grossed out or creeped out, but it was written to sound like an anecdote. It's a story about a prince of darkness, is it not? Not an episode of The Simpsons. <br /><br />I thought that her constantly calling him ex-boyfriend completely ruined and emasculated his character. Why don't you just call him Vlad? But she made it sound like he was some nerdy boy next door. <br /><br />Here are some of "WTH" lines:<br /><br />"Come on, I silently urged. Drill, baby, drill!"<br />"I'd soon smell like eau de slut."<br /><br />Then, there was a reason why Vlad brought her back to Romania for the second time.<br /><br />"If I do nothing when someone attempts to blow up and then kidnap my former lover, my enemies will think I'm weak and attack more of my people."<br /><br />But that is the complete apposite. Your enemies will think you are week if you try to hide every ex lover you ever had. It shows your weakness. Isn't that what they do, exploit them? The author needed to come up with a better reason for him to bring her with him, because this one didn't make any sense.<br /><br />Then, the scene where her sister slapped her. Is that the first thing you do after you find out your sister Is alive?<br />Don't even get me started on the whole wedding thing. It was beyond silly. <br />First, it was to late, then too soon and then not soon enough.<br />Suddenly the I love you's started flying left and right, and the proposal out of the blue. And, the wedding, which had to happen the same day. The dress got designed and made the same day. Vlad also managed to invite 2000 people in that short amount of time. One day!<br /><br />- END OF SPOILERS -<br /><br />They managed to completely forget that there was a killer on a loose, hungry for revenge.<br />The only characters I liked was Vlad and her father, who was a man of reason. I didn't finished the book, I stopped at 61% because I just couldn't take anymore of that silliness.<br /><br />I'm sorry to say, but I won't be reading anymore books in the series. But I hear that Jeanine's Frost Night Huntress series is quite good, I'll go and try that instead.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13095398133571948733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer542175767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7059520119371586405"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410579i/805251.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'd rather bleed to death."<br/>"If you were anyone else, those would be your last words."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>3.5 stars.</b> Maybe we're not quite at the point of pure Vlad depth but at least this time we got to see more tyranny at work.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Two vampires hung from the spiked silver chains embedded in the rock, a third impaled in front of them.<br/>"That's sick, I breathed."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Nobody probably cares about that except for me, I'm guessing. It's hard for me to imagine though, to figure out how gruesome Vlad should b</span>
  <span id="freeText7059520119371586405" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410579i/805251.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'd rather bleed to death."<br>"If you were anyone else, those would be your last words."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>3.5 stars.</b> Maybe we're not quite at the point of pure Vlad depth but at least this time we got to see more tyranny at work.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Two vampires hung from the spiked silver chains embedded in the rock, a third impaled in front of them.<br>"That's sick, I breathed."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Nobody probably cares about that except for me, I'm guessing. It's hard for me to imagine though, to figure out how gruesome Vlad should be portrayed, while he's still somehow supposed to be a love interest. <br><br>Leila seems to handle her prince of darkness just fine. She isn't one for sugar coating things. I can get behind that. Do I think she's taking everything in stride a bit too easily? Perhaps. While she realizes what he's done, does she really get it? Seeing the bigger picture through visions would have had me headed for the hills!<br><br>This wasn't the most action-packed book from Frost. There were some story lulls, I thought, but the getting was good enough for me to overlook a few lazy moments. The magic from the first few Night Huntress books still isn't there yet and the chemistry isn't quite at the Cat and Bones level, but there was a mini version of the infamous chapter 32 which happened after a big turning point in Leila's life. It was verrah nice. You'll just have to experience it for yourself if you want to know!<br><br>Even though Vlad and Leila are still stumbling through their feelings, there were still plenty of moments which stood out.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I can barely stand the sight of you because you're more beautiful than I've allowed myself to remember."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Leila has a bit of the Cat possessiveness and insecurity (she even had an inner voice *facepalm*). I wasn't real thrilled to see this. <br><br>I can't say that I found <i>Twice Tempted</i> to be the tightest-written second installment for a series but after a few just okay books, this worked fine for what I wanted to read in the moment. I'm looking forward to what's up next for these new partners in crime.<br><br>But please, no more "love is a drug" crap. I get enough of it in my contemporaries. <i>His embrace was my drug of choice, and as any addict knew, one sampling was too many - and a thousand never enough.</i> Boo. </span>

<div id="review_1098381571" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1098381571" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1098381571?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16432884654994688352"><b>Some spoilers here</b><br/>Twice Tempted is 2nd book in the Night Prince Series which is set in Jeanine Frost’s Night Huntress world and continues Vlad & Leila’s love story….which is still going thru some “bumpy” times.<br/><br/>Vlad is still a commitment phobe…struggling to let go of the demons in his past and giving in to his feelings for Leila.<br/><br/>Leila wants more than just being Vlad’s bedmate and when he offers her immortality instead of telling her that he loves her….she decides that’s it….leave Romania and go b</span>
  <span id="freeText16432884654994688352" style="display:none"><b>Some spoilers here</b><br>Twice Tempted is 2nd book in the Night Prince Series which is set in Jeanine Frost’s Night Huntress world and continues Vlad &amp; Leila’s love story….which is still going thru some “bumpy” times.<br><br>Vlad is still a commitment phobe…struggling to let go of the demons in his past and giving in to his feelings for Leila.<br><br>Leila wants more than just being Vlad’s bedmate and when he offers her immortality instead of telling her that he loves her….she decides that’s it….leave Romania and go back to her carnival home.<br><br>But soon Leila finds herself being targeted by an unknown forces, she finds herself unable to trust who her friends are and even if she can trust Vlad.<br>Fast paced action …..and lots of things happen in this story…<br><br>More about Vlad’s past and the history with his father<br><br>Vlad finally realizing how much Leila means to him…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438637126i/15737700.png" alt=" photo afae7509-c88e-496e-ae0c-abc9361b74fb_zpsnuwb7kfr.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>Leila turning into a vampire<br><br>Leila’s magical powers<br><br>And…..of course the wedding….OMG…so amazing..<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438637126i/15737701.jpg" alt=" photo boundbyflames-stepback-for-blog_zpsbytuwv4n.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> I really liked this book. Lost myself into the story and loved reading Vlad &amp; Leila’s love story….it’s impossible not to root for their HEA…<br><br>I am so looking forward to the next book!!<br><br>My favourite quote:<br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438637126i/15737702.jpg" alt=" photo 30b1bb54bef613d4b22ecd7cfa4ad83a_zpsjitqjltg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText2613971023882524483" style="display:none">One of the things I love about this author are her great one-liner beginning sentences that instantly engage you into the story<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Flying at high speeds through a forest is less dangerous than it looks. At least that´s what I told mysef the few imes I opened my eyes.” </i>

Adapting to their new circumstances and of course gotta fight the new bad guy<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I caught up to him instead. “What part of ‘we do this together’ did you translate as ‘leave Leila behind’?” I hissed, keeping my voice down since we weren’t the only ones with supernatural hearing.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><u>The more I read about Leila, the more I love her.</u> I’m use to more reckless characters but she is more a plotter of schemes which I quickly learned to love as well. In general, I would begin with Cat’s series then follow up with <b>Vlad&amp;Leila’s hot steamy dangerous epic adventure</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1818936066306893250"><b>
  <i>Fantastic!!!!!</i>
</b> Loved it!! Jeaniene Frost never disappoints. I loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7039218.Once_Burned__Night_Prince___1_' title='Once Burned (Night Prince, #1) by Jeaniene Frost' rel='nofollow noopener'>Once Burned</a> but I have to say <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125234.Twice_Tempted__Night_Prince___2_' title='Twice Tempted (Night Prince, #2) by Jeaniene Frost' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twice Tempted</a> is even better!!!<br/><br/><u>Book description:</u><br/><i>Dating the Prince of Darkness has its challenges...<br/>Leila's psychic abilities have been failing her, and now she isn't sure what the future holds. If that weren't enough, her lover, Vlad, has been acting distant. Though Leila is a mere mortal, she's also a modern woman who refuses to accept the cold shoulder treatment forever–especially from the dar</i></span>
  <span id="freeText1818936066306893250" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Fantastic!!!!!</i>
</b> Loved it!! Jeaniene Frost never disappoints. I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7039218.Once_Burned__Night_Prince___1_" title="Once Burned (Night Prince, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Once Burned</a> but I have to say <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125234.Twice_Tempted__Night_Prince___2_" title="Twice Tempted (Night Prince, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Twice Tempted</a> is even better!!!<br><br><u>Book description:</u><br><i>Dating the Prince of Darkness has its challenges...<br>Leila's psychic abilities have been failing her, and now she isn't sure what the future holds. If that weren't enough, her lover, Vlad, has been acting distant. Though Leila is a mere mortal, she's also a modern woman who refuses to accept the cold shoulder treatment forever–especially from the darkly handsome vampire who still won't admit that he loves her."</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“You should be afraid. Very afraid. Before, I told you if you wanted to end things between us, I would let you go, but, Leila"--his voice deepened--"I lied.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“No one feels like you do, so every brush of your skin is a cruel reminder of what I’ve lost. I can barely stand the sight of you because you’re more beautiful than I’ve allowed myself to remember, and when I cut that wire off Maximus and smelled you all over him, I wanted to kill him more than I’ve wanted to kill anyone in my life, yet I couldn’t because of my promise to you.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“If you introduce yourself to anyone as Mrs. Dracula, I'll bite you in a manner you won't enjoy.”</i>
</b><br><br>I felt <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7039218.Once_Burned__Night_Prince___1_" title="Once Burned (Night Prince, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Once Burned</a> was more about Leila and her POV <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125234.Twice_Tempted__Night_Prince___2_" title="Twice Tempted (Night Prince, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Twice Tempted</a> was all Vlad and we see the Vlad Tepesh we know and love from the "Night Huntress/Night Huntress World" novels. I cannot wait for book 3!! <br><br><br> <a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/albums/z369/dshewey1/?action=view&amp;current=305991_555746467792029_1186630448_n-1_zps3b7f7388.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379789223i/519944.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Reread on: 9.22.20</span>

<div id="review_570153065" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/570153065" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/570153065?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=trashy-romance-novel">trashy-romance-novel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer570153065" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17737728071587629632">I've said it before, but I'm betting a lot of you boys didn't believe me.<br/>So I'm gonna say it again:<br/><b>
  <i>When there's a vampire in a Paranormal Romance...he will eventually chomp on the heroine's Happy Bean!</i>
</b><br/>Case in point: <i><br/>Page 282 -<br/>All thought cleared my mind when his fangs replaced his tongue, piercing my clitoris instead of licking it.</i><br/><br/><b>Ta-da!</b><br/>Of course that has nothing to do with the review, but I thought you guys might like to know what exactly your ladies are reading. Word to the wise, though. S</span>
  <span id="freeText17737728071587629632" style="display:none">I've said it before, but I'm betting a lot of you boys didn't believe me.<br />So I'm gonna say it again:<br /><b>
  <i>When there's a vampire in a Paranormal Romance...he will eventually chomp on the heroine's Happy Bean!</i>
</b><br />Case in point: <i><br />Page 282 -<br />All thought cleared my mind when his fangs replaced his tongue, piercing my clitoris instead of licking it.</i><br /><br /><b>Ta-da!</b><br />Of course that has nothing to do with the review, but I thought you guys might like to know what exactly your ladies are reading. Word to the wise, though. Some things only work in the fantasy world of books. I wouldn't suggest you try that little trick out at home. You're not a sexy vampire, you (hopefully) don't have fangs, and I doubt many women will appreciate someone chewing on their sensitive bits.<br />Just sayin'.<br /><br />So I normally don't venture into the world of PNR much anymore, but I make an exception for Jeaniene Frost. Most of her stuff is rooted in Urban Fantasy, and there's always a great underlying story being told to go along with all of the lovey-dovey stuff.<br />Her Night Prince series is a spin-off of the Cat and Bones series (aka the Night Huntress series), and it features my favorite character, Vlad. I still like the Cat and Bones books, but every time Vlad makes an appearance, he kicks up the story a few notches.<br /><br />I have to admit that he's not <i>quite</i> as cool in his own series. Maybe that's because he isn't playing off of Bones? Not sure. At any rate, this was still a solid story, and a good addition to the Night Prince storyline.<br />I saw some other reviews that thought Leila got a bit whiny in this one, but I didn't think she was annoying. I thought she was justified in asking for <i>more</i> out of their relationship. Whatever. To each his own.<br /><br />For PNR with a good plot, you can't beat Frost. <br />I'll definitely read the next book when it comes out!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17737728071587629632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_571285306" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/571285306" />
    <a title="The BookChick " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick"><img alt="The BookChick " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546023730p2/6190526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/571285306?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The BookChick " class="user" itemprop="url" name="The BookChick " href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick">The BookChick </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16133809-twice-tempted">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=recommend-to-others">recommend-to-others</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=bad-boys-you-love">bad-boys-you-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=read-again">read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=jeaniene-frost">jeaniene-frost</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer571285306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11058162027564236307"><b>My Rating:</b> ❤❤❤❤❤ <blockquote> EXCELLENT: The characteristics of a 5 star story include: an awesome story; and, I love everything about the story — characters, plot, and story elements. I would definitely read it again and I would highly recommend it to a friend and rave about it often.</blockquote> <b>Initial Reaction:</b> The. Best. Story. Ever. Jeaniene Frost manages to top herself every time!!!<br/><br/><b>Rating's Breakdown:</b><blockquote> <b>Quality of writing:</b> Excellent<br/><br/><b>Pace:</b> Fast and fluid<br/><br/><b>Characters:</b> Dynamic! Absolutely captivating. We see one of hist</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11058162027564236307" style="display:none"><b>My Rating:</b> ❤❤❤❤❤ <blockquote> EXCELLENT: The characteristics of a 5 star story include: an awesome story; and, I love everything about the story — characters, plot, and story elements. I would definitely read it again and I would highly recommend it to a friend and rave about it often.</blockquote> <b>Initial Reaction:</b> The. Best. Story. Ever. Jeaniene Frost manages to top herself every time!!!<br><br><b>Rating's Breakdown:</b><blockquote> <b>Quality of writing:</b> Excellent<br><br><b>Pace:</b> Fast and fluid<br><br><b>Characters:</b> Dynamic! Absolutely captivating. We see one of history's fictional doppleganger's at his finest. Vlad is the ultimate definition of a lover and a fighter and Leila was no slacker in the kick a$$ heroine department. She almost rivals Cat in her fierceness. All of the characters were well thought out in how they acted as individuals and together.<br> <br><b>Plot development:</b> Superb. Highly detailed and full of intricacies that kept the reader fully engaged in the story.<br><br><b>Story line:</b> Exceptional! This is one of Frost's best stories and I love all of her books.<br><br><b>Enjoyability:</b> Clearly there is something wrong if you've reached this point in this brief review and haven't realized that I loved this story *smile*.<br><br>My emotions were all over the map while reading <i>Twice Tempted</i>.<br><br>&lt;--<b>At the Beginning</b> (because I was so happy to be reading it)<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414883ra/818453.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>When Leila left...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411821ra/809483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>When Vlad came after her...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/530603.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>When Maximus left...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399653ra/773655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>--&gt;<b>At the End</b> (because I was sorry to see it end).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414883ra/818454.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Heat Level:</b> Smoking hotttttt...quite literally<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/651621.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote> <b>My Thoughts:</b> <br><br><i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125234.Twice_Tempted__Night_Prince___2_" title="Twice Tempted (Night Prince, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Twice Tempted</a>
</i> picks up immediately where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7039218.Once_Burned__Night_Prince___1_" title="Once Burned (Night Prince, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Once Burned</a> left off. Without providing any details about the story, because I'm strongly recommend that you pick up your own copy, I can say that this was one of Ms. Frost's best stories. This story was high-def all the way -- the imagery, the character depth, and their emotions and motivations. At almost 400 pages, <i>Twice Tempted</i> never lulled or dragged and was full throttle from start to finish. I don't know how Frost does it but I am amazed that she continues to write stories at such a superbly consistent level. Many of my favorite authors lose me after a while because their stories become trite or repetitive but never have I experienced that kind of disappointment with Frost. <br><br><i>Twice Tempted</i> was a BRILLIANT story. Read it! Love it!<br><br>Bravo Ms. Frost! Bravo!!!<blockquote>
<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401246ra/778529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Visit The BookChick Blog</b> <a href="http://bookchickwithkick.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388474i/748995.jpg" alt=" photo 480761_117447861780253_1600570465_n_zps49e00d53.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote></span>
